## Abumi Zaku

- Image: https://i.imgur.com/zCdcIJ8.png

- Chakra profile: Random:4, Blood:2
- Role tags: damage, defense, chakra-control, counter, aoe, invisible

### Description

Abumi Zaku is one of the three sound genin sent to the chuunin exams. He was surgically altered with hollow tubes in his arms, allowing him to create waves of compressed air.

### Skills

#### Air Cutter

- Cooldown: 0
- Energy: `Blood`
- Energy readable: Bloodline
- Classes: `Physical`, `Ranged`, `Instant`
- Image: https://i.imgur.com/tm12H2k.png

Zaku fires a blast of supersonic air at one enemy, dealing 25 damage to them. The following turn, Zaku can use 'Extreme Air Cutter'.

#### Wall of Air

- Cooldown: 2
- Energy: `Random`
- Energy readable: Random
- Classes: `Physical`, `Instant`, `Unique`
- Image: https://i.imgur.com/upWnlDl.png

Zaku alters his air wave to protect one ally for 1 turn. The first harmful skill used on that ally will be countered. If successful, Zaku will instantly apply 'Air Cutter' on the countered enemy. This skill is invisible.

#### Extreme Air Cutter

- Cooldown: 0
- Energy: `Blood` + `Random` + `Random`
- Energy readable: Bloodline + Random + Random
- Classes: `Physical`, `Ranged`, `Instant`, `Unique`
- Image: https://i.imgur.com/Yo7IQNe.png

Zaku boosts his air waves to a frightening level and deals 45 damage to all enemies. Afterwards, Zaku gains 1 random chakra.

- Cooldown: 4
- Energy: `Random`
- Energy readable: Random
- Classes: `Chakra`, `Instant`
- Image: https://i.imgur.com/xssUpbi.png

This skill makes Abumi Zaku invulnerable for 1 turn.

Shino directs his chakra draining bugs to one enemy, dealing 20 affliction damage and stealing 1 taijutsu or genjutsu chakra from their chakra pool. If this skill successfully steals a chakra from the opponent, this skill will cost an extra random chakra for 1 turn.

- Cooldown: 2
- Energy: None
- Energy readable: None
- Classes: `Physical`, `Ranged`, `Instant`, `Unique`, `Affliction`
- Image: https://i.imgur.com/MRWPHSi.png

Shino directs one of his female bugs to attach itself. For 4 turns, 'Chakra Leach' will deal 5 additional damage to one enemy. During this time, if that enemy uses a new harmful skill, they will deal 5 less non-affliction damage for 1 turn. This skill stacks.

#### Bug Wall

- Cooldown: 5
- Energy: `Blood` + `Random`
- Energy readable: Bloodline + Random
- Classes: `Physical`, `Instant`, `Unique`
- Image: https://i.imgur.com/Zvu9ydw.png

Shino calls millions of bugs to create a wall protecting himself and his allies and granting them 20 points of permanent destructible defense.

- Classes: `Chakra`, `Affliction`, `Melee`, `Unique`, `Instant`

Shino infects one enemy with a small bug. 3 turns after this skill has been used, the bug bursts out, dealing 30 affliction damage to them and activating all other copies of this skill on that enemy. This skill is invisible.

- Energy readable: Random
- Classes: `Physical`, `Instant`, `Unique`
- Image: https://i.imgur.com/5G2uYVn.png

This skill makes Zetsu (S) invulnerable for 1 turn.
